❯ There is a slight change :                                                    
                                                                                
  Read PRODUCT.md in full. That is the source of truth for this entire project. 
  Do not create any files, do not run any commands, do not install anything.    
                                                                                
  Here is what you need to understand before we begin:                          
                                                                                
  This project is called Workbench Studio v1.1. It is a Natural Language Schema 
  Migration tool built for the OpenAI × Outskill Builder Hackathon. A           
  developer types a plain-English feature request and the tool generates a full 
  vertical slice across four layers of a codebase — SQL migration, ORM model,   
  Express routes, and a React component — using Codex CLI as the AI engine.     
                                                                                
  The AI engine is Codex CLI installed globally on this machine. It is spawned  
  as a child process from the agent backend. It is not the OpenAI HTTP API. It  
  is not any other AI provider. It reads the sandbox codebase directly and      
  writes files to disk.                                                         
                                                                                
  The project has three applications running simultaneously. The sandbox app on 
  port 5000 is the target codebase. The agent engine on port 4000 orchestrates  
  Codex CLI and streams progress via Server-Sent Events. Workbench Studio on    
  port 3000 is the React frontend with a three-panel UI showing the file tree,  
  Monaco diff explorer, sandbox iframe, and thinking console.                   
                                                                                
  When I say "session two begins" that is your signal to start building. Until  
  then, acknowledge that you have read and understood PRODUCT.md and wait for   
  my instruction.

       14 +---                                                           
       15  
       16 +## What It Does                                               
       17 +                                                              
       18 +A developer types a plain-English feature request (e.g. "Add a
          + ratings and reviews system") and the tool generates a full ve
          +rtical slice across four layers:                              
       19 +1. SQL database migration                                     
       20 +2. JavaScript ORM model                                       
       21 +3. Express.js API routes                                      
       22 +4. React UI component stub                                    
       23 +                                                              
       24 +All four files are generated by Codex CLI, applied to the live
          + sandbox app, and immediately visible in an embedded preview. 
       25 +                                                              
       26  ---
       27  
       18 -## What's Being Built                                         
       28 +## AI Engine — Codex CLI (NOT the OpenAI HTTP API)            
       29  
       20 -Three apps working together:                                  
       30 +**Critical:** The agent does NOT call the OpenAI HTTP API. It 
          +does NOT use the `openai` npm SDK for code generation. It spaw
          +ns Codex CLI as a local child process.                        
       31  
       22 -1. **Sandbox App** (:5000) — Mock e-commerce SaaS (Express + b
          -etter-sqlite3 + Vanilla JS). Tables: users, products, orders. 
          -The "before" codebase the AI extends.                         
       23 -2. **Agent Engine** (:4000) — Node.js + Express server orchest
          -rating OpenAI API calls. Parses sandbox, runs 4-step pipeline,
          - writes generated files to disk.                              
       24 -3. **Developer Studio** (:3000) — React 18 + Vite 5 frontend. 
          -3-panel workspace: file tree + demo ideas (left), Monaco diff 
          -explorer (center), sandbox iframe + thinking console (right). 
       25 -4. **Offline Demo Cache** — Pre-generated JSON for two demo sc
          -enarios (Referral System, Ratings & Reviews). Bypasses API ent
          -irely on stage. Toggled via Demo/Live AI switch.              
       32 +```js                                                         
       33 +spawn('codex', ['--full-auto', '--quiet', prompt], { cwd: SAND
          +BOX })                                                        
       34 +```                                                           
       35  
       36 +- `@openai/codex` must be installed globally: `npm install -g 
          +@openai/codex`                                                
       37 +- `--full-auto` is mandatory — without it Codex hangs waiting 
          +for approval                                                  
       38 +- `--quiet` suppresses interactive TUI, outputs plain text to 
          +stdout                                                        
       39 +- `cwd` is always set to the sandbox directory so Codex reads 
          +the existing codebase as context automatically                
       40 +- Codex writes generated files directly to disk; the agent det
          +ects changes via before/after directory snapshots             
       41 +- `OPENAI_API_KEY` is still needed in `.env` — used by Codex C
          +LI internally for authentication                              
       42 +

       57 +- AI Engine: Codex CLI (`@openai/codex`, global)              
       58 +- Studio Frontend: React 18 + Vite 5                          
       59 +- Styling: TailwindCSS 3                                      
       60 +- Code Diff Display: Monaco Editor (`@monaco-editor/react`)

          +e vs after Codex runs)

       57 -## Four-Layer Pipeline (per feature request)                  
       67 +---                                                           
       68  
       59 -1. **SCAN** — Read schema.sql, db.js, server.js. Build context
          - object.                                                      
       60 -2. **DESIGN** — gpt-4o generates SQL migration from feature in
          -tent.                                                         
       61 -3. **GENERATE** — Generate ORM model, Express route, React com
          -ponent.                                                       
       62 -4. **VALIDATE** — Write all files to disk, run SQL migration, 
          -restart sandbox.                                              
       69 +## Pipeline (4 steps)                                         
       70  
       64 -Four separate API calls (not one) for better output quality an
          -d real-time streaming to the thinking console.                
       71 +1. **SCAN** — parser snapshots sandbox dir (before state)     
       72 +2. **GENERATE** — agent spawns Codex CLI; every stdout line em
          +itted as SSE `CODEX` event to Studio                          
       73 +3. **VALIDATE** — parser snapshots again; diffs before vs afte
          +r to find new/changed files                                   
       74 +4. **APPLY** (user-triggered) — Studio POSTs to `/api/apply`; 
          +applier runs `.migration.sql` against sandbox.db; Studio reloa
          +ds iframe

  Here is what I know:

  Workbench Studio v1.1 — the AI engine is Codex CLI (@openai/codex, global
  install), spawned as a child process with cwd set to the sandbox directory. It
  is not the OpenAI HTTP API. It is not any npm SDK call. Codex reads the
  codebase directly and writes files to disk. The agent detects what changed via
  before/after directory snapshots.

  The three apps are Sandbox (:5000), Agent Engine (:4000), and Workbench Studio
  (:3000). One prompt file (feature.prompt.js) builds the natural language
  instruction for Codex. SSE streams every line of Codex stdout to the
  ThinkingConsole in real time. The primary demo scenario — "Add a ratings and
  reviews system" — must be bulletproof.

❯ # Workbench Studio v1.1 — Phase 1 PRD                                         
  ## Agent Engine & Codex CLI Pipeline                                          
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Objective                                                                  
                                                                                
  Build the entire agent backend. By the end of Phase 1, typing a feature       
  request and hitting the synthesize endpoint must trigger Codex CLI, stream    
  real output back via SSE, detect what files were generated, and return a      
  structured diff object. The Studio does not need to be wired yet — all        
  verification in this phase happens via terminal and curl.                     
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Prerequisites                                                              
                                                                                
  Phase 0 must be fully complete before starting Phase 1. Verify:               
                                                                                
  ```bash                                                                       
  curl http://localhost:5000/api/health                                         
  # must return { "status": "ok", "port": 5000 }                                
                                                                                
  codex --version                                                               
  # must return a version number — not "command not found"                      
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  If either fails, stop and resolve Phase 0 issues first.                       
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Deliverables                                                               
                                                                                
  Phase 1 is complete when all of the following work:                           
                                                                                
  1. `agent/parser.js` — snapshots and diffs the sandbox directory correctly    
  2. `agent/prompts/feature.prompt.js` — builds a precise, file-named Codex CLI 
  prompt                                                                        
  3. `agent/orchestrator.js` — spawns Codex CLI, streams stdout, returns file   
  diffs                                                                         
  4. `agent/applier.js` — runs SQL migration against sandbox.db without errors  
  5. `agent/index.js` — Express server on port 4000 with `/api/synthesize`,     
  `/api/apply`, `/api/reset`, `/api/files` endpoints all working                
  6. A curl test against `/api/synthesize` in demo mode returns a complete      
  changes object                                                                
  7. A curl test against `/api/apply` successfully runs the migration and

      14 +                                                               
      15 +function snapshotDir(dir) {                                    
      16 +  const snapshot = {};                                         
      17 +                                                               
      18 +  function walk(currentDir, prefix = '') {                     
      19 +    const entries = fs.readdirSync(currentDir);                
      20 +    for (const entry of entries) {                             
      21 +      if (entry.startsWith('.')) continue;                     
      22 +      if (entry === 'node_modules') continue;                  
      23 +      if (entry === 'public') continue;                        
      24 +                                                               
      25 +      const fullPath = path.join(currentDir, entry);           
      26 +      const stat     = fs.statSync(fullPath);                  
      27 +      const key      = prefix ? `${prefix}/${entry}` : entry;  
      28 +                                                               
      29 +      if (stat.isDirectory()) {                                
      30 +        walk(fullPath, key);                                   
      31 +      } else if (stat.isFile()) {                              
      32 +        snapshot[key] = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8');     
      33 +      }                                                        
      34 +    }                                                          
      35 +  }                                                            
      36 +                                                               
      37 +  walk(dir);                                                   
      38 +  return snapshot;                                             
      39 +}                                                              
      40 +                                                               
      41 +function diffSnapshots(before, after) {                        
      42 +  const changes = {};                                          
      43 +                                                               
      44 +  for (const [file, content] of Object.entries(after)) {       
      45 +    const isBaseline = BASELINE_FILES.has(path.basename(file));
      46 +    if (isBaseline) continue;                                  
      47 +                                                               
      48 +    const existed = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(before
         +, file);                                                       
      49 +    const changed = existed && before[file] !== content;       
      50 +    const isNew   = !existed;                                  
      51 +                                                               
      52 +    if (isNew || changed) {                                    
      53 +      changes[file] = {                                        
      54 +        original:  existed ? before[file] : '',                
      55 +        generated: content,                                    
      56 +        isNew,                                                 
      57 +        language:  detectLanguage(file)                        
      58 +      };                                                       
      59 +    }                                                          
      60 +  }                                                            
      61 +                                                               
      62 +  return changes;                                              
      63 +}                                                              
      64 +                                                               
      65 +function detectLanguage(filename) {                            
      66 +  const ext = path.extname(filename).toLowerCase();            
      67 +  const map  = {                                               
      68 +    '.sql':  'sql',                                            
      69 +    '.js':   'javascript',                                     
      70 +    '.jsx':  'javascript',                                     
      71 +    '.ts':   'typescript',                                     
      72 +    '.tsx':  'typescript',                                     
      73 +    '.json': 'json',                                           
      74 +    '.md':   'markdown',                                       
      75 +    '.css':  'css',                                            
      76 +    '.html': 'html'                                            
      77 +  };                                                           
      78 +  return map[ext] || 'plaintext';                              
      79 +}                                                              
      80 +                                                               
      81 +function getSandboxPath() {                                    
      82 +  return SANDBOX;                                              
      83 +}                                                              
      84 +                                                               
      85 +module.exports = { snapshotDir, diffSnapshots, getSandboxPath, 
         +SANDBOX };

● Write(agent\orchestrator.js)
  ⎿  Added 88 lines, removed 2 lines
       1 -// Orchestrator — spawns Codex CLI and streams output          
       2 -// Implemented in Phase 1                                      
       1 +const { spawn }                               = require('child_
         +process');                                                     
       2 +const { snapshotDir, diffSnapshots, SANDBOX } = require('./pars
         +er');                                                          
       3 +const buildPrompt                             = require('./prom
         +pts/feature.prompt');                                          
       4 +                                                               
       5 +const CODEX_TIMEOUT_MS = 120000;                               
       6 +                                                               
       7 +function spawnCodex(prompt, onOutput) {                        
       8 +  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {                    
       9 +    let proc;                                                  
      10 +                                                               
      11 +    try {                                                      
      12 +      proc = spawn('codex', ['--full-auto', '--quiet', prompt],
         + {                                                             
      13 +        cwd: SANDBOX,                                          
      14 +        env: { ...process.env },                               
      15 +        shell: false                                           
      16 +      });                                                      
      17 +    } catch (err) {                                            
      18 +      return reject(new Error('Failed to spawn Codex CLI. Is it
         + installed globally? Run: npm install -g @openai/codex'));     
      19 +    }                                                          
      20 +                                                               
      21 +    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {                         
      22 +      proc.kill('SIGTERM');                                    
      23 +      reject(new Error('Codex CLI timed out after 2 minutes'));
      24 +    }, CODEX_TIMEOUT_MS);                                      
      25 +                                                               
      26 +    proc.stdout.on('data', data => {                           
      27 +      const lines = data.toString().split('\n').filter(l => l.t
         +rim());                                                        
      28 +      for (const line of lines) {                              
      29 +        onOutput(line.trim());                                 
      30 +      }                                                        
      31 +    });                                                        
      32 +                                                               
      33 +    proc.stderr.on('data', data => {                           
      34 +      const lines = data.toString().split('\n').filter(l => l.t
         +rim());                                                        
      35 +      for (const line of lines) {                              
      36 +        onOutput(`[stderr] ${line.trim()}`);                   
      37 +      }                                                        
      38 +    });                                                        
      39 +                                                               
      40 +    proc.on('close', code => {                                 
      41 +      clearTimeout(timeout);                                   
      42 +      if (code === 0 || code === null) {                       
      43 +        resolve();                                             
      44 +      } else {                                                 
      45 +        reject(new Error(`Codex CLI exited with code ${code}`))
         +;                                                              
      46 +      }                                                        
      47 +    });                                                        
      48 +                                                               
      49 +    proc.on('error', err => {                                  
      50 +      clearTimeout(timeout);                                   
      51 +      if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {                             
      52 +        reject(new Error('Codex CLI not found. Run: npm install
         + -g @openai/codex'));                                          
      53 +      } else {                                                 
      54 +        reject(err);                                           
      55 +      }                                                        
      56 +    });                                                        
      57 +  });                                                          
      58 +}                                                              
      59 +                                                               
      60 +async function orchestrate(feature, onStep) {                  
      61 +  const sleep = ms => new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms));     
      62 +                                                               
      63 +  await onStep('SCAN', 'Reading sandbox codebase...');         
      64 +  const before = snapshotDir(SANDBOX);                         
      65 +  await sleep(400);                                            
      66 +                                                               
      67 +  await onStep('GENERATE', 'Spawning Codex CLI...');           
      68 +  const prompt = buildPrompt(feature, SANDBOX);                
      69 +                                                               
      70 +  await spawnCodex(prompt, line => {                           
      71 +    onStep('CODEX', line);                                     
      72 +  });                                                          
      73 +                                                               
      74 +  await onStep('VALIDATE', 'Detecting generated files...');    
      75 +  const after   = snapshotDir(SANDBOX);                        
      76 +  const changes = diffSnapshots(before, after);                
      77 +                                                               
      78 +  const fileCount = Object.keys(changes).length;               
      79 +  await onStep('VALIDATE', `Found ${fileCount} generated file${
         +fileCount === 1 ? '' : 's'}`);                                 
      80 +                                                               
      81 +  if (fileCount === 0) {                                       
      82 +    throw new Error('Codex CLI completed but no new files were 
         +detected. Check the prompt or Codex CLI output.');             
      83 +  }                                                            
      84 +                                                               
      85 +  return changes;                                              
      86 +}                                                              
      87 +                                                               
      88 +module.exports = { orchestrate };

       5 +function applyMigration(changes) {                             
       6 +  const sqlEntry = Object.entries(changes)                     
       7 +    .find(([filename]) => filename.endsWith('.migration.sql'));
       8 +                                                               
       9 +  if (!sqlEntry) {                                             
      10 +    return { applied: false, reason: 'No migration file found i
         +n changes' };                                                  
      11 +  }                                                            
      12 +                                                               
      13 +  const [filename, { generated }] = sqlEntry;                  
      14 +                                                               
      15 +  if (!generated || !generated.trim()) {

         +};

      18 +

      20 +

      22 +    db.exec(generated);                                        
      23 +    return { applied: true, file: filename };                  
      24 +  } catch (err) {                                              
      25 +    throw new Error(`Migration failed: ${err.message}`);       
      26 +  } finally {                                                  
      27 +    db.close();                                                
      28 +  }                                                            
      29 +}                                                              
      30 +                                                               
      31 +function resetGeneratedTables(tableNames = []) {

      33 +                                                               
      34 +  const db = new Database(path.join(SANDBOX, 'sandbox.db'));   
      35 +  try {                                                        
      36 +    for (const table of tableNames) {                          
      37 +      db.exec(`DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ${table}`);                
      38 +    }                                                          
      39 +  } finally {                                                  
      40 +    db.close();                                                
      41 +  }                                                            
      42 +}

       59 +app.get('/api/synthesize', async (req, res) => {

      102 +    }                                                         
      103 +                                                              
      104 +    emit('complete', { changes });                            
      105 +    res.end();                                                
      106 +                                                              
      107 +  } catch (err) {                                             
      108 +    emit('error', { message: err.message });                  
      109 +    res.end();                                                
      110 +  }                                                           
      111 +});                                                           
      112 +                                                              
      113 +/**                                                           
      114 + * POST /api/apply                                            
      115 + * Body: { changes: { ... } }                                 
      116 + */                                                           
      117 +app.post('/api/apply', (req, res) => {                        
      118 +  const { changes } = req.body;                               
      119 +                                                              
      120 +  if (!changes || typeof changes !== 'object') {              
      121 +    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'changes object is re
          +quired' });                                                   
      122 +  }                                                           
      123 +                                                              
      124 +  try {                                                       
      125 +    const result = applyMigration(changes);                   
      126 +    res.json({ success: true, ...result });                   
      127 +  } catch (err) {                                             
      128 +    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message 
          +});                                                           
      129 +  }                                                           
      130 +});                                                           
      131 +                                                              
      132 +/**                                                           
      133 + * POST /api/reset                                            
      134 + * Body: { tables: ['reviews', 'referrals'] }                 
      135 + */                                                           
      136 +app.post('/api/reset', (req, res) => {                        
      137 +  try {                                                       
      138 +    const { tables = ['reviews', 'referrals', 'ratings'] } = r
          +eq.body || {};                                                
      139 +                                                              
      140 +    const generated = getGeneratedFiles();                    
      141 +    let removed = 0;                                          
      142 +    for (const f of generated) {                              
      143 +      fs.unlinkSync(path.join(SANDBOX, f));                   
      144 +      removed++;                                              
      145 +    }                                                         
      146 +                                                              
      147 +    resetGeneratedTables(tables);                             
      148 +                                                              
      149 +    res.json({ success: true, filesRemoved: removed, tablesDro
          +pped: tables });                                              
      150 +  } catch (err) {                                             
      151 +    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message 
          +});                                                           
      152 +  }                                                           
      153 +});                                                           
      154 +                                                              
      155 +/**                                                           
      156 + * GET /api/files                                             
      157 + */                                                           
      158 +app.get('/api/files', (req, res) => {                         
      159 +  try {                                                       
      160 +    const snapshot  = snapshotDir(SANDBOX);                   
      161 +    const generated = getGeneratedFiles();                    
      162 +    res.json({                                                
      163 +      all:      Object.keys(snapshot),                        
      164 +      generated,                                              
      165 +      baseline: ['schema.sql', 'db.js', 'server.js']          
      166 +    });                                                       
      167 +  } catch (err) {                                             
      168 +    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });             
      169 +  }                                                           
      170 +});                                                           
      171 +                                                              
      172 +/**                                                           
      173 + * GET /api/health                                            
      174 + */                                                           
      175 +app.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {                        
      176 +  res.json({ status: 'ok', port: PORT, mode: 'agent' });      
      177 +});                                                           
      178 +                                                              
      179 +// ─── Start ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
          +──────────────────                                            
      180 +                                                              
      181 +app.listen(PORT, () => {                                      
      182 +  console.log(`Agent Engine running at http://localhost:${PORT
          +}`);                                                          
      183 +  console.log(`Sandbox path: ${SANDBOX}`);                    
      184 +});

❯ # Workbench Studio v1.1 — Phase 2 and 3 PRD                                   
  ## The Developer Studio UI — Complete Implementation                          
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Objective                                                                  
                                                                                
  Build the complete Workbench Studio frontend. By the end of Phase 2 and 3 ,   
  the full three-panel UI is functional, the SSE pipeline is wired end-to-end,  
  the Monaco diff explorer shows generated file diffs, the thinking console     
  streams Codex CLI output in real time, and the sandbox iframe updates live    
  after Apply Slice. A judge must be able to sit down, type a feature request,  
  and watch the entire pipeline run without any developer intervention.         
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Prerequisites                                                              
                                                                                
  Phase 1 must be fully complete before starting Phase 2. Verify:

       1 +const BASE = import.meta.env.VITE_AGENT_URL || 'http://localhos
         +t:4000';                                                       
       2 +                                                               
       3 +export async function applySlice(changes) {                    
       4 +  const res = await fetch(`${BASE}/api/apply`, {               
       5 +    method:  'POST',                                           
       6 +    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },           
       7 +    body:    JSON.stringify({ changes })                       
       8 +  });                                                          
       9 +  if (!res.ok) {                                               
      10 +    const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: 'Unknown
         + error' }));                                                   
      11 +    throw new Error(err.error || 'Apply failed');              
      12 +  }                                                            
      13 +  return res.json();                                           
      14 +}                                                              
      15 +                                                               
      16 +export async function resetSandbox(tables = ['reviews', 'referr
         +als', 'ratings']) {                                            
      17 +  const res = await fetch(`${BASE}/api/reset`, {               
      18 +    method:  'POST',                                           
      19 +    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },           
      20 +    body:    JSON.stringify({ tables })                        
      21 +  });                                                          
      22 +  if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Reset failed');                
      23 +  return res.json();                                           
      24 +}                                                              
      25 +                                                               
      26 +export async function getFiles() {                             
      27 +  const res = await fetch(`${BASE}/api/files`);                
      28 +  if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch files');       
      29 +  return res.json();                                           
      30 +}                                                              
      31 +                                                               
      32 +export function buildSynthesizeURL(feature, mode) {            
      33 +  const params = new URLSearchParams({ feature, mode });       
      34 +  return `${BASE}/api/synthesize?${params.toString()}`;        
      35 +}

       1 -// useSSE — EventSource hook                                   
       2 -// Implemented in Phase 1                                      
       3 -export function useSSE() {}                                    
       1 +import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';         
       2 +import { buildSynthesizeURL } from '../lib/api';               
       3 +                                                               
       4 +export function useSSE() {                                     
       5 +  const [steps,     setSteps]     = useState([]);              
       6 +  const [changes,   setChanges]   = useState(null);            
       7 +  const [isRunning, setIsRunning] = useState(false);           
       8 +  const [error,     setError]     = useState(null);            
       9 +  const esRef = useRef(null);                                  
      10 +                                                               
      11 +  const synthesize = useCallback((feature, mode) => {          
      12 +    if (esRef.current) {                                       
      13 +      esRef.current.close();                                   
      14 +      esRef.current = null;                                    
      15 +    }                                                          
      16 +                                                               
      17 +    setSteps([]);                                              
      18 +    setChanges(null);                                          
      19 +    setError(null);                                            
      20 +    setIsRunning(true);                                        
      21 +                                                               
      22 +    const url = buildSynthesizeURL(feature, mode);             
      23 +    const es  = new EventSource(url);                          
      24 +    esRef.current = es;                                        
      25 +                                                               
      26 +    es.addEventListener('step', e => {                         
      27 +      try {                                                    
      28 +        const data = JSON.parse(e.data);                       
      29 +        setSteps(prev => [...prev, {                           
      30 +          ...data,                                             
      31 +          timestamp: new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {  
      32 +            hour12:  false,                                    
      33 +            hour:    '2-digit',                                
      34 +            minute:  '2-digit',                                
      35 +            second:  '2-digit'                                 
      36 +          })                                                   
      37 +        }]);                                                   
      38 +      } catch (_) {}                                           
      39 +    });                                                        
      40 +                                                               
      41 +    es.addEventListener('complete', e => {                     
      42 +      try {                                                    
      43 +        const data = JSON.parse(e.data);                       
      44 +        setChanges(data.changes);                              
      45 +      } catch (_) {}                                           
      46 +      setIsRunning(false);                                     
      47 +      es.close();                                              
      48 +      esRef.current = null;                                    
      49 +    });                                                        
      50 +                                                               
      51 +    es.addEventListener('error', e => {                        
      52 +      try {                                                    
      53 +        const data = JSON.parse(e.data);                       
      54 +        setError(data.message || 'Generation failed');         
      55 +      } catch (_) {                                            
      56 +        setError('Connection to agent lost');                  
      57 +      }                                                        
      58 +      setIsRunning(false);                                     
      59 +      es.close();                                              
      60 +      esRef.current = null;                                    
      61 +    });                                                        
      62 +                                                               
      63 +    es.onerror = () => {                                       
      64 +      setError('Agent connection failed. Is the agent running o
         +n port 4000?');                                                
      65 +      setIsRunning(false);                                     
      66 +      es.close();                                              
      67 +      esRef.current = null;                                    
      68 +    };                                                         
      69 +  }, []);                                                      
      70 +                                                               
      71 +  const cancel = useCallback(() => {                           
      72 +    if (esRef.current) {                                       
      73 +      esRef.current.close();                                   
      74 +      esRef.current = null;                                    
      75 +    }                                                          
      76 +    setIsRunning(false);                                       
      77 +  }, []);                                                      
      78 +                                                               
      79 +  const reset = useCallback(() => {                            
      80 +    setSteps([]);                                              
      81 +    setChanges(null);                                          
      82 +    setError(null);                                            
      83 +    setIsRunning(false);                                       
      84 +  }, []);                                                      
      85 +                                                               
      86 +  return { steps, changes, isRunning, error, synthesize, cancel
         +, reset };                                                     
      87 +}

❯ # Workbench Studio v1.1 — Phase 4 PRD                                         
  ## Offline Cache, Live Codex CLI Testing & Demo Hardening                     
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Objective                                                                  
                                                                                
  Make the product bulletproof for a live presentation. By the end of Phase 4,  
  the offline demo cache is verified and complete, the live Codex CLI pipeline  
  runs end-to-end at least once successfully, all failure modes are handled     
  gracefully, the Reset Sandbox cycle works flawlessly, and the full demo       
  scenario runs without any developer intervention from a cold start.           
                                                                                
  This phase has zero new features. It is entirely about reliability.           
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Prerequisites                                                              
                                                                                
  Phases 0, 1, and 2+3 must be fully complete before starting Phase 4. Verify:  
                                                                                
  ```bash                                                                       
  # All three servers start cleanly                                             
  npm run dev                                                                   
                                                                                
  # Agent health                                                                
  curl http://localhost:4000/api/health                                         
  # { "status": "ok", "port": 4000, "mode": "agent" }                           
                                                                                
  # Studio loads with no console errors                                         
  # Open localhost:3000 in browser — full three-panel UI must be visible        
                                                                                
  # Demo mode synthesis completes end-to-end                                    
  # Click "Add Ratings & Reviews" → Synthesize Slice → four file tabs appear    
  # Apply Slice → sandbox iframe reloads                                        
  # Reset Sandbox → all state clears                                            
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  All five checks must pass. If any fail, stop and fix Phase 2+3 issues first.  
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Deliverables                                                               
                                                                                
  Phase 4 is complete when all of the following are confirmed:                  
                                                                                
  1. Both cache files contain real, verified, working content                   
  2. Demo mode runs the full pipeline in under 5 seconds with no errors         
  3. Live Codex CLI mode runs successfully at least once end-to-end             
  4. Live mode auto-saves to cache after a successful run                       
  5. All four generated files from the live run are syntactically valid         
  6. Apply Slice works on both cached and live-generated content                
  7. Reset Sandbox cleanly restores original state after both demo and live     
  runs                                                                          
  8. All error states display cleanly in the UI — no blank screens, no uncaught 
  exceptions                                                                    
  9. The full nine-step smoke test from PRODUCT.md passes from a cold start     
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Step 1 — Verify Existing Cache Files                                       
                                                                                
  The cache files were written manually in Phase 1. Before testing anything     
  else, verify they parse correctly and contain all four required entries.      
                                                                                
  ### Step 1a — Parse Check                                                     
                                                                                
  Run from the agent directory:                                                 
                                                                                
  ```bash

  const rs = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('cache/referral-system.json', 'utf8')); 
                                                                                
  console.log('=== ratings-reviews.json ===');                                  
  console.log('Feature:', rr.feature);                                          
  console.log('Files:', Object.keys(rr.chang                                    
  ──── (487 lines hidden) ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── 
   sandbox/*.component.jsx                                                      
                                                                                
  # Verify node_modules exist                                                   
  ls sandbox/node_modules > /dev/null || (cd sandbox && npm install)            
  ls agent/node_modules   > /dev/null || (cd agent   && npm install)            
  ls studio/node_modules  > /dev/null || (cd studio  && npm install)            
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Step 9b — Cold Start                                                      
                                                                                
  ```bash                                                                       
  # From root, start everything fresh                                           
  npm run dev                                                                   
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Step 9c — Run the Smoke Test                                              
                                                                                
  Open a browser that has never visited localhost:3000 in this session (use     
  incognito if needed). Run the full nine-step smoke test from Step 5. Every    
  step must pass without any setup beyond `npm run dev`.                        
                                                                                
  If any step fails on a cold start, it will fail on stage. Fix it now.         
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Phase 4 Completion Checklist                                               
                                                                                
  - [ ] Both cache files parse correctly and contain four file entries each     
  - [ ] SQL migrations in both cache files are valid and create tables without  
  errors                                                                        
  - [ ] Fuzzy cache loader handles slight variations in feature wording         
  - [ ] Codex CLI `--version` returns a version number on the demo machine      
  - [ ] Isolated Codex CLI test creates a file in /tmp/codex-test successfully  
  - [ ] Live pipeline curl test emits CODEX events showing real CLI output      
  - [ ] Live run auto-saves updated cache file with correct generatedAt         
  timestamp

  - [ ] `api/reload` endpoint mounts generated routes without restarting        
  sandbox

  - [ ] Full nine-step smoke test passes in Live AI mode                        
  - [ ] All six failure modes display clean errors — no blank screens or        
  uncaught exceptions

  - [ ] Referral system cache verified working in Demo mode                     
  - [ ] Cold start test passes — npm run dev → full demo works with zero setup

  ### Step 9b — Cold Start                                                      
                                                                                
  ```bash                                                                       
  # From root, start everything fresh                                           
  npm run dev                                                                   
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Step 9c — Run the Smoke Test                                              
                                                                                
  Open a browser that has never visited localhost:3000 in this session (use     
  incognito if needed). Run the full nine-step smoke test from Step 5. Every    
  step must pass without any setup beyond `npm run dev`.                        
                                                                                
  If any step fails on a cold start, it will fail on stage. Fix it now.         
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Phase 4 Completion Checklist                                               
                                                                                
  - [ ] Both cache files parse correctly and contain four file entries each     
  - [ ] SQL migrations in both cache files are valid and create tables without  
  errors                                                                        
  - [ ] Fuzzy cache loader handles slight variations in feature wording         
  - [ ] Codex CLI `--version` returns a version number on the demo machine      
  - [ ] Isolated Codex CLI test creates a file in /tmp/codex-test successfully  
  - [ ] Live pipeline curl test emits CODEX events showing real CLI output      
  - [ ] Live run auto-saves updated cache file with correct generatedAt         
  timestamp                                                                     
  - [ ] Generated files appear on disk in sandbox/ after a live run             
  - [ ] `api/reload` endpoint mounts generated routes without restarting        
  sandbox                                                                       
  - [ ] `localhost:5000/api/reviews` returns `[]` after Apply Slice             
  - [ ] Full nine-step smoke test passes in Demo mode                           
  - [ ] Full nine-step smoke test passes in Live AI mode                        
  - [ ] All six failure modes display clean errors — no blank screens or        
  uncaught exceptions                                                           
  - [ ] Demo mode timing feels correct at presentation pace                     
  - [ ] Referral system cache verified working in Demo mode                     
  - [ ] Cold start test passes — npm run dev → full demo works with zero setup  
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## What Phase 4 Does Not Include                                              
                                                                                
  Do not implement any of the following in this phase:                          
                                                                                
  - UI animations, transitions, or visual polish — Phase 5                      
  - README or documentation — Phase 5                                           
  - Demo video recording — Phase 5                                              
  - Any new features or UI components — out of scope                            
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## On Completion                                                              
                                                                                
  Report the following:                                                         
                                                                                
  1. Confirmation that all checklist items pass                                 
  2. Output of the cold start smoke test — list which of the nine steps passed  
  and how long the full sequence took                                           
  3. Which Codex CLI flags worked on this machine for the live pipeline         
  4. Current state of both cache files — generatedAt timestamps and file counts 
                                                                                
  Then stop. Phase 5 begins in the next session.

       46 +// ─── Dynamic generated-route mounting ──────────────────────
          +─────────────────                                             
       47 +//                                                            
       48 +// Each generated *.routes.js file is mounted under two paths 
          +so the demo                                                   
       49 +// works regardless of how a downstream component constructs U
          +RLs:                                                          
       50 +//   1. /api/<full-feature-slug>      (derived from the filena
          +me)                                                           
       51 +//   2. /api/<table-noun>             (last segment of the slu
          +g — e.g. "reviews")                                           
       52 +//                                                            
       53 +// We track the routers we've mounted in a stack so reload cal
          +ls can swap                                                   
       54 +// them out without polluting Express's middleware chain.     
       55 +const mountedRouters = [];                                    
       56 +                                                              
       57 +function clearGeneratedMounts() {                             
       58 +  while (mountedRouters.length) mountedRouters.pop();         
       59 +  // Remove the previously-installed dynamic routers from the 
          +stack.                                                        
       60 +  app._router && (app._router.stack = app._router.stack.filter
          +(

          +th - 1];

  Codex CLI flags that worked on this machine

  Codex CLI v0.133 changed flags. The PRD's --full-auto --quiet no longer exist.
  Final working invocation:

  spawn(process.execPath, [
    CODEX_SCRIPT,                                  // resolved to 
  ~/AppData/Roaming/npm/.../codex.js
    'exec',
    '--dangerously-bypass-approvals-and-sandbox',  // v0.133 equivalent of 
  legacy --full-auto
    '--skip-git-repo-check',                       // sandbox/ isn't a git repo
    '-'                                            // read prompt from stdin
  ], { cwd: SANDBOX, stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'] })

  Bypassing the .cmd shim and spawning node directly on codex.js sidesteps Node
  24's EINVAL guard against .cmd/.bat execution and the Git-bash cmd.exe ENOENT
  issue. Codex emits most output on stderr (banner, diffs) — the orchestrator
  now treats stderr as normal CODEX output without the [stderr] prefix.

❯ # Workbench Studio v1.1 — Phase 5 PRD                                         
  ## Polish, Demo Preparation & Final Submission                                
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Objective                                                                  
                                                                                
  Take a working, hardened product and make it presentation-ready. By the end   
  of Phase 5, the UI is visually polished, the demo script is rehearsed, the    
  README is complete, a demo video is recorded, and the final submission        
  package is ready. No new features. No architecture changes. Every hour in     
  this phase is spent making what already works look and feel exceptional.      
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Prerequisites                                                              
                                                                                
  Phase 4 must be fully complete before starting Phase 5. Verify:               
                                                                                
  ```bash                                                                       
  # Cold start passes — this is non-negotiable                                  
  rm -f sandbox/sandbox.db                                                      
  rm -f sandbox/*.migration.sql sandbox/*.model.js sandbox/*.routes.js          
  sandbox/*.component.jsx

  # All nine steps must pass before Phase 5 begins

  it. Do not start Phase 5 with a broken cold start.

  ### Step 1a — Header                                                          
                                                                                
  The header is the first thing judges see. It must communicate the product     
  name, version, and status instantly.                                          
                                                                                
  Add an animated status indicator that shows which server processes are        
  running. After the Studio loads, it should ping the agent health endpoint and 
  show a green connected dot if the agent is up, or a red dot if it is not      
  reachable:                                                                    
                                                                                
  ```jsx                                                                        
  // Add to Header component in App.jsx                                         
  function AgentStatus() {                                                      
    const [connected, setConnected] = React.useState(null);                     
                                                                                
    React.useEffect(() => {                                                     
      const check = async () => {                                               
        try {                                                                   
          await fetch('http://localhost:4000/api/health');                      
          setConnected(true);                                                   
        } catch {                                                               
          setConnected(false);                                                  
        }                                                                       
      };                                                                        
      check();                                                                  
      const interval = setInterval(check, 5000);                                
      return () => clearInterval(interval);                                     
    }, []);                                                                     
                                                                                
    if (connected === null) return nul

      206 +    return () => { cancelled = true; clearInterval(interval); 
          +};

      209 +  if (connected === null) return null;

      211 +  return (

          +──────────────                                                
      404 +    let lastFeatureKey = '';                                  
      405 +                                                              
      406 +    async function refreshFeatures() {                        
      407 +      try {                                                   
      408 +        const data = await fetch('/api/extensions').then(r => 
          +r.json());                                                    
      409 +        const features = data.features || [];                 
      410 +        const key = features.map(f => f.table).sort().join(','
          +);                                                            
      411 +        if (key === lastFeatureKey) return;                   
      412 +        lastFeatureKey = key;                                 
      413 +                                                              
      414 +        const root = document.getElementById('features');     
      415 +        root.innerHTML = '';                                  
      416 +        for (const feature of features) {                     
      417 +          const host = document.createElement('div');         
      418 +          root.appendChild(host);                             
      419 +          const renderer = renderers[feature.table];          
      420 +          if (renderer) renderer(host);                       
      421 +          else          renderGeneric(host, feature);         
      422 +        }                                                     
      423 +      } catch (_) {}                                          
      424 +    }                                                         
      425 +                                                              
      426 +    loadProducts();                                           
      427 +    refreshFeatures();                                        
      428 +    setInterval(refreshFeatures, 2000);                       
      429    </script>
      430  </body>
      431  </html>

  └───────────────────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────┘

  What the user will see in the sandbox iframe:

  Before Apply Slice: ShopBase product grid only.

  After Apply Slice for ratings: a ⭐ Ratings & Reviews [JUST ADDED] panel
  slides in above the products with a rating dropdown, comment field, Submit
  button, and a live list of submitted reviews showing stars + comment +
  timestamp.

  After Apply Slice for referrals: a 🎁 Referral System [JUST ADDED] panel
  appears with "Generate referral code" button (shows the generated code in a
  styled badge) and a "Redeem" form.

  After Reset: panels disappear, only the product grid remains.

  Three changes summary:
  1. sandbox/server.js — added /api/extensions endpoint reporting
  currently-mounted feature tables (Express 5 compatible)
  2. sandbox/public/index.html — polls /api/extensions every 2s, renders
  purpose-built UI for reviews and referrals plus a generic fallback for any
  other table
  3. sandbox/db.js — seeded a second user so referral redemption works (FK
  constraint requires both referrer + referred user IDs to exist)

  The Studio's sandbox iframe will now visibly transform when Apply Slice runs —
  "I can use it right now" in the demo script is no longer just words.

          +t not found' });                                              
       73 +                                                              
       74 +    const total  = product.price * quantity;                  
       75 +    const result = db.prepare(                                
       76 +      'INSERT INTO orders (user_id, product_id, quantity, tota
          +l) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)'                                       
       77 +    ).run(user_id, product_id, quantity, total);              
       78 +                                                              
       79 +    res.status(201).json({ id: result.lastInsertRowid, total }
          +);                                                            
       80 +  } catch (err) {                                             
       81 +    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });             
       82 +  }                                                           
       83 +});                                                           
       84 +                                                              
       85 +// Features endpoint — lists currently-mounted generated route
          +s for the sandbox UI banner                                   
       86 +app.get('/api/features', (req, res) => {                      
       87 +  try {                                                       
       88 +    const routeFiles = fs.readdirSync(__dirname)              
       89 +      .filter(f => f.endsWith('.routes.js'))                  
       90 +      .map(f => {                                             
       91 +        const slug     = f.replace('.routes.js', '');         
       92 +        const endpoint = '/api/' + slug;                      
       93 +        const label    = slug.split('-').map(w => w.charAt(0).
          +toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(' ');                        
       94 +        return { slug, endpoint, label, file: f };            
       95 +      });                                                     
       96 +    res.json(routeFiles);                                     
       97 +  } catch (err) {                                             
       98 +    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });             
       99 +  }                                                           
      100 +});                                                           
      101 +                                                              
      102  // Health check
      103  app.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {
      104    res.json({ status: 'ok', port: 5000 });

      662 +    function timeAgo(dateStr) {                               
      663 +      const d    = new Date(dateStr);                         
      664 +      const diff = (Date.now() - d.getTime()) / 1000;         
      665 +      if (diff < 60)    return 'just now';                    
      666 +      if (diff < 3600)  return Math.floor(diff / 60)   + 'm ag
          +o';                                                           
      667 +      if (diff < 86400) return Math.floor(diff / 3600) + 'h ag
          +o';                                                           
      668 +      return d.toLocaleDateString();
